I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder crashes with NPE/IOOBE when candidates is null or empty
## Describe the bug

`GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.append()` accesses `partialResponse.candidates().get(0)` on line 62 without checking if `candidates()` is null or empty.

When the Gemini API returns a response with no candidates (e.g. due to safety filtering, quota errors, or malformed responses), this causes:
- `NullPointerException` if `candidates()` is null
- `IndexOutOfBoundsException` if `candidates()` is an empty list

## Log and Stack trace

```
java.lang.NullPointerException
    at dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.append(GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.java:62)
```

or

```
java.lang.IndexOutOfBoundsException: Index 0 out of bounds for length 0
    at java.base/java.util.ImmutableCollections$ListN.get(ImmutableCollections.java:XXX)
    at dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.append(GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.java:62)
```

## How To Reproduce

Send a request to the Gemini API via `GoogleAiGeminiStreamingChatModel` that triggers a safety filter or results in an empty candidates list. The streaming callback will crash instead of gracefully returning empty.

## Expected behavior

The `append()` method should check for null/empty candidates and return an empty `TextAndTools` result, consistent with how the Vertex AI Gemini module's `StreamingChatResponseBuilder` already handles this case (see `langchain4j-vertex-ai-gemini/.../StreamingChatResponseBuilder.java` line 30-31).

## Environment
- Langchain4j version: 1.0.0-beta1+
- Java version: 17+
- Spring Boot version: N/A


</pr_description>

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.googleai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.FinishReasonMapper.fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.PartsAndContentsMapper.fromGPartsToAiMessage;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason.TOOL_EXECUTION;
     7	
     8	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
     9	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiCandidate;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiUsageMetadata;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    15	import java.util.ArrayList;
    16	import java.util.List;
    17	import java.util.Map;
    18	import java.util.Optional;
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * A builder class for constructing streaming responses from Gemini AI model.
    24	 * This class accumulates partial responses and builds a final response.
    25	 */
    26	class GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    27	
    28	    private final boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    29	    private final Boolean returnThinking;
    30	
    31	    private final StringBuilder contentBuilder;
    32	    private final StringBuilder thoughtBuilder;
    33	    private final Map<String, Object> attributes = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    34	    private final List<ToolExecutionRequest> functionCalls;
    35	
    36	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    37	    private final AtomicReference<String> modelName = new AtomicReference<>();
    38	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    39	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    40	
    41	    GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput, Boolean returnThinking) {
    42	        this.includeCodeExecutionOutput = includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    43	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    44	        this.contentBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    45	        this.thoughtBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    46	        this.functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    record TextAndTools(Optional<String> maybeText, Optional<String> maybeThought, List<ToolExecutionRequest> tools) {}
    50	
    51	    /**
    52	     * Appends a partial response to the builder.
    53	     *
    54	     * @param partialResponse the partial response from Gemini AI
    55	     * @return an Optional containing the text of the partial response, or empty if no valid text
    56	     */
    57	    TextAndTools append(GeminiGenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
    58	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    59	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        GeminiCandidate firstCandidate = partialResponse.candidates().get(0);
    63	
    64	        updateId(partialResponse);
    65	        updateModelName(partialResponse);
    66	        updateFinishReason(firstCandidate);
    67	        updateTokenUsage(partialResponse.usageMetadata());
    68	
    69	        GeminiContent content = firstCandidate.content();
    70	        if (content == null || content.parts() == null) {
    71	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        AiMessage message = fromGPartsToAiMessage(content.parts(), includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
    75	        updateContentAndFunctionCalls(message);
    76	
    77	        return new TextAndTools(
    78	                Optional.ofNullable(message.text()),
    79	                Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()),
    80	                message.toolExecutionRequests());
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    /**
    84	     * Builds the complete response from all accumulated partial responses.
    85	     *
    86	     * @return a Response object containing the complete AiMessage, token usage, and finish reason
    87	     */
    88	    ChatResponse build() {
    89	        AiMessage aiMessage = createAiMessage();
    90	        return ChatResponse.builder()
    91	                .aiMessage(aiMessage)
    92	                .metadata(GoogleAiGeminiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
    93	                        .id(id.get())
    94	                        .modelName(modelName.get())
    95	                        .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
    96	                        .finishReason(aiMessage.hasToolExecutionRequests() ? TOOL_EXECUTION : finishReason.get())
    97	                        .build())
    98	                .build();
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    private void updateId(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.responseId())) {
   103	            id.set(response.responseId());
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
   109	            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
   114	        if (usageMetadata != null) {
   115	            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
   116	                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
   117	                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
   118	                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
   119	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
   120	        }
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
   124	        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
   125	            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
   126	        }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
   130	        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
   131	        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
   132	        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
   133	        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
   134	            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
   139	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   140	        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();
   141	
   142	        return AiMessage.builder()
   143	                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
   144	                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
   145	                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
   146	                .attributes(attributes)
   147	                .build();
   148	    }
   149	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.vertexai.gemini;
     2	
     3	import com.google.cloud.vertexai.api.*;
     4	import com.google.cloud.vertexai.generativeai.ResponseHandler;
     5	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
     7	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;
     8	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
     9	
    10	import java.util.ArrayList;
    11	import java.util.List;
    12	import java.util.stream.Collectors;
    13	
    14	class StreamingChatResponseBuilder {
    15	
    16	    private final StringBuffer contentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    17	
    18	    private final List<FunctionCall> functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    19	
    20	    private volatile TokenUsage tokenUsage;
    21	    private volatile FinishReason finishReason;
    22	
    23	    record TextAndFunctions(String text, List<FunctionCall> functionCalls) {}
    24	
    25	    TextAndFunctions append(GenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
    26	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    27	            return new TextAndFunctions(null, List.of());
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        List<Candidate> candidates = partialResponse.getCandidatesList();
    31	        if (candidates.isEmpty() || candidates.get(0) == null) {
    32	            return new TextAndFunctions(null, List.of());
    33	        }
    34	
    35	        String text = ResponseHandler.getText(partialResponse);
    36	        contentBuilder.append(text);
    37	
    38	        List<FunctionCall> functionCalls = candidates.stream()
    39	                .map(Candidate::getContent)
    40	                .map(Content::getPartsList)
    41	                .flatMap(List::stream)
    42	                .filter(Part::hasFunctionCall)
    43	                .map(Part::getFunctionCall)
    44	                .collect(Collectors.toList());
    45	
    46	        if (!functionCalls.isEmpty()) {
    47	            this.functionCalls.addAll(functionCalls);
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        if (partialResponse.hasUsageMetadata()) {
    51	            tokenUsage = TokenUsageMapper.map(partialResponse.getUsageMetadata());
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        Candidate.FinishReason finishReason = ResponseHandler.getFinishReason(partialResponse);
    55	        if (finishReason != null) {
    56	            this.finishReason = FinishReasonMapper.map(finishReason);
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        return new TextAndFunctions(text, functionCalls);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    Response<AiMessage> build() {
    63	        if (!functionCalls.isEmpty()) {
    64	            return Response.from(
    65	                AiMessage.from(FunctionCallHelper.fromFunctionCalls(functionCalls)),
    66	                tokenUsage,
    67	                finishReason
    68	            );
    69	        } else {
    70	            return Response.from(
    71	                AiMessage.from(contentBuilder.toString()),
    72	                tokenUsage,
    73	                finishReason
    74	            );
    75	        }
    76	    }
    77	}

    47	class GeminiService {

    49	    private static final String GEMINI_AI_ENDPOINT = "https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta";
    50	    private static final String API_KEY_HEADER_NAME = "x-goog-api-key";
    51	    private static final Duration DEFAULT_CONNECT_TIMEOUT = ofSeconds(15);
    52	    private static final Duration DEFAULT_READ_TIMEOUT = ofSeconds(60);
    53	
    54	    private final HttpClient httpClient;
    55	    private final String baseUrl;
    56	    private final String apiKey;
    57	
    58	    enum BatchOperationType {
    59	        BATCH_GENERATE_CONTENT("batchGenerateContent"),
    60	        ASYNC_BATCH_EMBED_CONTENT("asyncBatchEmbedContent");
    61	
    62	        private final String value;
    63	
    64	        BatchOperationType(String value) {
    65	            this.value = value;
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        public String getValue() {
    69	            return value;
    70	        }
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    GeminiService(
    74	            final @Nullable HttpClientBuilder httpClientBuilder,
    75	            final String apiKey,
    76	            final String baseUrl,
    77	            final boolean logRequestsAndResponses,
    78	            final boolean logRequests,
    79	            final boolean logResponses,
    80	            final Logger logger,
    81	            final Duration timeout) {
    82	        this.apiKey = apiKey;
    83	        this.baseUrl = getOrDefault(baseUrl, GeminiService.GEMINI_AI_ENDPOINT);
    84	        final var builder = getOrDefault(httpClientBuilder, HttpClientBuilderLoader::loadHttpClientBuilder);
    85	        HttpClient httpClient = builder.connectTimeout(
    86	                        firstNotNull("connectTimeout", timeout, builder.connectTimeout(), DEFAULT_CONNECT_TIMEOUT))
    87	                .readTimeout(firstNotNull("readTimeout", timeout, builder.readTimeout(), DEFAULT_READ_TIMEOUT))
    88	                .build();
    89	
    90	        if (logRequestsAndResponses || logResponses || logRequests) {
    91	            this.httpClient = new LoggingHttpClient(
    92	                    httpClient,
    93	                    logRequestsAndResponses || logRequests,
    94	                    logRequestsAndResponses || logResponses,
    95	                    logger);
    96	        } else {
    97	            this.httpClient = httpClient;
    98	        }
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    GeminiGenerateContentResponse generateContent(String modelName, GeminiGenerateContentRequest request) {
   102	        String url = String.format("%s/models/%s:generateContent", baseUrl, modelName);
   103	        return sendRequest(url, apiKey, request, GeminiGenerateContentResponse.class);
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   107	    <REQ, RESP> BatchRequestResponse.Operation<RESP> batchCreate(
   108	            String modelName, BatchRequestResponse.BatchCreateRequest<REQ> request, BatchOperationType operationType) {
   109	        return (BatchRequestResponse.Operation<RESP>) sendRequest(
   110	                String.format("%s/models/%s:%s", baseUrl, modelName, operationType.value),
   111	                apiKey,
   112	                request,
   113	                BatchRequestResponse.Operation.class);
   114	    }

   119	                String.format("%s/models/%s:%s", baseUrl, modelName, operationType.value),
   120	                apiKey,

   128	                String.format("%s/%s", baseUrl, operationName),
   129	                apiKey,
   130	                null,
   131	                BatchRequestResponse.Operation.class,

   148	                baseUrl + "/batches",
   149	                new StringPair("pageSize", pageSize != null ? String.valueOf(pageSize) : null),
   150	                new StringPair("pageToken", pageToken));
   151	        return sendRequest(url, apiKey, null, ListOperationsResponse.class, GET);

   177	    void generateContentStream(
   178	            String modelName,
   179	            GeminiGenerateContentRequest request,
   180	            boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput,
   181	            Boolean returnThinking,
   182	            StreamingChatResponseHandler handler) {
   183	        String url = String.format("%s/models/%s:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse", baseUrl, modelName);
   184	        streamRequest(url, apiKey, request, includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking, handler);
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    private <T> T sendRequest(String url, String apiKey, @Nullable Object requestBody, Class<T> responseType) {
   188	        return sendRequest(url, apiKey, requestBody, responseType, POST);
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    private <T> T sendRequest(
   192	            String url, String apiKey, @Nullable Object requestBody, Class<T> responseType, HttpMethod httpMethod) {
   193	        HttpRequest request = buildHttpRequest(url, apiKey, requestBody, httpMethod);
   194	        return fromJson(httpClient.execute(request).body(), responseType);
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    private void streamRequest(
   198	            String url,
   199	            String apiKey,
   200	            Object requestBody,
   201	            boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput,
   202	            Boolean returnThinking,
   203	            StreamingChatResponseHandler handler) {
   204	        HttpRequest httpRequest = buildHttpRequest(url, apiKey, requestBody, POST);
   205	
   206	        GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder responseBuilder =
   207	                new GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
   208	
   209	        httpClient.execute(httpRequest, new ServerSentEventListener() {
   210	
   211	            AtomicInteger toolIndex = new AtomicInteger(0);
   212	            volatile StreamingHandle streamingHandle;
   213	
   214	            @Override
   215	            public void onEvent(ServerSentEvent event) {
   216	                onEvent(event, new ServerSentEventContext(new CancellationUnsupportedHandle()));
   217	            }
   218	
   219	            @Override
   220	            public void onEvent(ServerSentEvent event, ServerSentEventContext context) {
   221	                if (streamingHandle == null) {
   222	                    streamingHandle = toStreamingHandle(context.parsingHandle());
   223	                }
   224	
   225	                GeminiGenerateContentResponse response = fromJson(event.data(), GeminiGenerateContentResponse.class);
   226	                GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder.TextAndTools textAndTools = responseBuilder.append(response);
   227	                textAndTools.maybeText().ifPresent(text -> {
   228	                    onPartialResponse(handler, text, streamingHandle);
   229	                });
   230	                textAndTools.maybeThought().ifPresent(thought -> {
   231	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(returnThinking)) {
   232	                        onPartialThinking(handler, thought, streamingHandle);
   233	                    } else if (returnThinking == null) {
   234	                        onPartialResponse(handler, thought, streamingHandle); // for backward compatibility
   235	                    }
   236	                });
   237	                for (ToolExecutionRequest tool : textAndTools.tools()) {
   238	                    CompleteToolCall completeToolCall = new CompleteToolCall(toolIndex.get(), tool);
   239	                    onCompleteToolCall(handler, completeToolCall);
   240	                    toolIndex.incrementAndGet();
   241	                }
   242	            }
   243	
   244	            @Override
   245	            public void onClose() {
   246	                if (streamingHandle == null || !streamingHandle.isCancelled()) {
   247	                    ChatResponse completeResponse = responseBuilder.build();
   248	                    onCompleteResponse(handler, completeResponse);
   249	                }
   250	            }
   251	
   252	            @Override
   253	            public void onError(Throwable error) {
   254	                RuntimeException mappedError = ExceptionMapper.DEFAULT.mapException(error);
   255	                withLoggingExceptions(() -> handler.onError(mappedError));
   256	            }
   257	        });
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    private HttpRequest buildHttpRequest(String url, String apiKey, @Nullable Object body, HttpMethod method) {
   261	        var builder = HttpRequest.builder()
   262	                .method(method)
   263	                .url(url)
   264	                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/json")
   265	                .addHeader("User-Agent", "LangChain4j");
   266	        if (apiKey != null) {
   267	            builder.addHeader(API_KEY_HEADER_NAME, apiKey);
   268	        }
   269	        if (body != null) {
   270	            builder.body(Json.toJson(body));
   271	        }
   272	        return builder.build();
   273	    }
   274	
   275	    private static String buildUrl(String baseUrl, StringPair... pairs) {
   276	        var queryParams = Stream.of(pairs)
   277	                .filter(pair -> pair.value != null)
   278	                .map(entry -> entry.key() + "=" + URLEncoder.encode(entry.value(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
   279	                .collect(Collectors.joining("&"));
   280	
   281	        return queryParams.isEmpty() ? baseUrl : baseUrl + "?" + queryParams;
   282	    }
   283	
   284	    private record StringPair(String key, @Nullable String value) {}
   285	}

     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason.TOOL_EXECUTION;
     7	
     8	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
     9	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiCandidate;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiUsageMetadata;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    15	import java.util.ArrayList;
    16	import java.util.List;
    17	import java.util.Map;
    18	import java.util.Optional;
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * A builder class for constructing streaming responses from Gemini AI model.
    24	 * This class accumulates partial responses and builds a final response.
    25	 */
    26	class GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    27	
    28	    private final boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    29	    private final Boolean returnThinking;
    30	
    31	    private final StringBuilder contentBuilder;
    32	    private final StringBuilder thoughtBuilder;
    33	    private final Map<String, Object> attributes = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    34	    private final List<ToolExecutionRequest> functionCalls;
    35	
    36	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    37	    private final AtomicReference<String> modelName = new AtomicReference<>();
    38	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    39	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    40	
    41	    GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput, Boolean returnThinking) {
    42	        this.includeCodeExecutionOutput = includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    43	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    44	        this.contentBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    45	        this.thoughtBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    46	        this.functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    record TextAndTools(Optional<String> maybeText, Optional<String> maybeThought, List<ToolExecutionRequest> tools) {}
    50	
    51	    /**
    52	     * Appends a partial response to the builder.
    53	     *
    54	     * @param partialResponse the partial response from Gemini AI
    55	     * @return an Optional containing the text of the partial response, or empty if no valid text
    56	     */
    57	    TextAndTools append(GeminiGenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
    58	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    59	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        GeminiCandidate firstCandidate = partialResponse.candidates().get(0);
    63	
    64	        updateId(partialResponse);
    65	        updateModelName(partialResponse);
    66	        updateFinishReason(firstCandidate);
    67	        updateTokenUsage(partialResponse.usageMetadata());
    68	
    69	        GeminiContent content = firstCandidate.content();
    70	        if (content == null || content.parts() == null) {
    71	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        AiMessage message = fromGPartsToAiMessage(content.parts(), includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
    75	        updateContentAndFunctionCalls(message);
    76	
    77	        return new TextAndTools(
    78	                Optional.ofNullable(message.text()),
    79	                Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()),
    80	                message.toolExecutionRequests());
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    /**
    84	     * Builds the complete response from all accumulated partial responses.
    85	     *
    86	     * @return a Response object containing the complete AiMessage, token usage, and finish reason
    87	     */
    88	    ChatResponse build() {
    89	        AiMessage aiMessage = createAiMessage();
    90	        return ChatResponse.builder()
    91	                .aiMessage(aiMessage)
    92	                .metadata(GoogleAiGeminiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
    93	                        .id(id.get())
    94	                        .modelName(modelName.get())
    95	                        .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
    96	                        .finishReason(aiMessage.hasToolExecutionRequests() ? TOOL_EXECUTION : finishReason.get())
    97	                        .build())
    98	                .build();
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    private void updateId(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.responseId())) {
   103	            id.set(response.responseId());
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
   109	            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
   114	        if (usageMetadata != null) {
   115	            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
   116	                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
   117	                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
   118	                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
   119	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
   120	        }
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
   124	        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
   125	            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
   126	        }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
   130	        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
   131	        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
   132	        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
   133	        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
   134	            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
   139	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   140	        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();
   141	
   142	        return AiMessage.builder()
   143	                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
   144	                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
   145	                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
   146	                .attributes(attributes)
   147	                .build();
   148	    }
   149	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.googleai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.FinishReasonMapper.fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.PartsAndContentsMapper.fromGPartsToAiMessage;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason.TOOL_EXECUTION;
     7	
     8	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
     9	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiCandidate;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiUsageMetadata;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    15	import java.util.ArrayList;
    16	import java.util.List;
    17	import java.util.Map;
    18	import java.util.Optional;
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * A builder class for constructing streaming responses from Gemini AI model.
    24	 * This class accumulates partial responses and builds a final response.
    25	 */
    26	class GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    27	
    28	    private final boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    29	    private final Boolean returnThinking;
    30	
    31	    private final StringBuilder contentBuilder;
    32	    private final StringBuilder thoughtBuilder;
    33	    private final Map<String, Object> attributes = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    34	    private final List<ToolExecutionRequest> functionCalls;
    35	
    36	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    37	    private final AtomicReference<String> modelName = new AtomicReference<>();
    38	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    39	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    40	
    41	    GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput, Boolean returnThinking) {
    42	        this.includeCodeExecutionOutput = includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    43	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    44	        this.contentBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    45	        this.thoughtBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    46	        this.functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    record TextAndTools(Optional<String> maybeText, Optional<String> maybeThought, List<ToolExecutionRequest> tools) {}
    50	
    51	    /**
    52	     * Appends a partial response to the builder.
    53	     *
    54	     * @param partialResponse the partial response from Gemini AI
    55	     * @return an Optional containing the text of the partial response, or empty if no valid text
    56	     */
    57	    TextAndTools append(GeminiGenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
    58	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    59	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        GeminiCandidate firstCandidate = partialResponse.candidates().get(0);
    63	
    64	        updateId(partialResponse);
    65	        updateModelName(partialResponse);
    66	        updateFinishReason(firstCandidate);
    67	        updateTokenUsage(partialResponse.usageMetadata());
    68	
    69	        GeminiContent content = firstCandidate.content();
    70	        if (content == null || content.parts() == null) {
    71	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        AiMessage message = fromGPartsToAiMessage(content.parts(), includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
    75	        updateContentAndFunctionCalls(message);
    76	
    77	        return new TextAndTools(
    78	                Optional.ofNullable(message.text()),
    79	                Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()),
    80	                message.toolExecutionRequests());
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    /**
    84	     * Builds the complete response from all accumulated partial responses.
    85	     *
    86	     * @return a Response object containing the complete AiMessage, token usage, and finish reason
    87	     */
    88	    ChatResponse build() {
    89	        AiMessage aiMessage = createAiMessage();
    90	        return ChatResponse.builder()
    91	                .aiMessage(aiMessage)
    92	                .metadata(GoogleAiGeminiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
    93	                        .id(id.get())
    94	                        .modelName(modelName.get())
    95	                        .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
    96	                        .finishReason(aiMessage.hasToolExecutionRequests() ? TOOL_EXECUTION : finishReason.get())
    97	                        .build())
    98	                .build();
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    private void updateId(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.responseId())) {
   103	            id.set(response.responseId());
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
   109	            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
   114	        if (usageMetadata != null) {
   115	            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
   116	                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
   117	                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
   118	                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
   119	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
   120	        }
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
   124	        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
   125	            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
   126	        }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
   130	        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
   131	        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
   132	        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
   133	        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
   134	            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
   139	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   140	        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();
   141	
   142	        return AiMessage.builder()
   143	                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
   144	                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
   145	                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
   146	                .attributes(attributes)
   147	                .build();
   148	    }
   149	}

   111	
   112	    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   113	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
   114	            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
   115	        }
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
   119	        if (usageMetadata != null) {
   120	            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
   121	                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
   122	                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
   123	                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
   124	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
   125	        }
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
   129	        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
   130	            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
   131	        }
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
   135	        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
   136	        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
   137	        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
   138	        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
   139	            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
   140	        }
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
   144	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   145	        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();
   146	
   147	        return AiMessage.builder()
   148	                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
   149	                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
   150	                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
   151	                .attributes(attributes)
   152	                .build();
   153	    }
   154	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.googleai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.FinishReasonMapper.fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.PartsAndContentsMapper.fromGPartsToAiMessage;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason.TOOL_EXECUTION;
     7	
     8	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
     9	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiCandidate;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiUsageMetadata;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    15	import java.util.ArrayList;
    16	import java.util.List;
    17	import java.util.Map;
    18	import java.util.Optional;
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * A builder class for constructing streaming responses from Gemini AI model.
    24	 * This class accumulates partial responses and builds a final response.
    25	 */
    26	class GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    27	
    28	    private final boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    29	    private final Boolean returnThinking;
    30	
    31	    private final StringBuilder contentBuilder;
    32	    private final StringBuilder thoughtBuilder;
    33	    private final Map<String, Object> attributes = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    34	    private final List<ToolExecutionRequest> functionCalls;
    35	
    36	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    37	    private final AtomicReference<String> modelName = new AtomicReference<>();
    38	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    39	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    40	
    41	    GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput, Boolean returnThinking) {
    42	        this.includeCodeExecutionOutput = includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    43	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    44	        this.contentBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    45	        this.thoughtBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    46	        this.functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    record TextAndTools(Optional<String> maybeText, Optional<String> maybeThought, List<ToolExecutionRequest> tools) {}
    50	
    51	    /**
    52	     * Appends a partial response to the builder.
    53	     *
    54	     * @param partialResponse the partial response from Gemini AI
    55	     * @return an Optional containing the text of the partial response, or empty if no valid text
    56	     */
    57	    TextAndTools append(GeminiGenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
    58	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    59	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        List<GeminiCandidate> candidates = partialResponse.candidates();
    63	        if (candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty() || candidates.get(0) == null) {
    64	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        GeminiCandidate firstCandidate = candidates.get(0);
    68	
    69	        updateId(partialResponse);
    70	        updateModelName(partialResponse);
    71	        updateFinishReason(firstCandidate);
    72	        updateTokenUsage(partialResponse.usageMetadata());
    73	
    74	        GeminiContent content = firstCandidate.content();
    75	        if (content == null || content.parts() == null) {
    76	            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        AiMessage message = fromGPartsToAiMessage(content.parts(), includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
    80	        updateContentAndFunctionCalls(message);
    81	
    82	        return new TextAndTools(
    83	                Optional.ofNullable(message.text()),
    84	                Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()),
    85	                message.toolExecutionRequests());
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    /**
    89	     * Builds the complete response from all accumulated partial responses.
    90	     *
    91	     * @return a Response object containing the complete AiMessage, token usage, and finish reason
    92	     */
    93	    ChatResponse build() {
    94	        AiMessage aiMessage = createAiMessage();
    95	        return ChatResponse.builder()
    96	                .aiMessage(aiMessage)
    97	                .metadata(GoogleAiGeminiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
    98	                        .id(id.get())
    99	                        .modelName(modelName.get())
   100	                        .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
   101	                        .finishReason(aiMessage.hasToolExecutionRequests() ? TOOL_EXECUTION : finishReason.get())
   102	                        .build())
   103	                .build();
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private void updateId(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   107	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.responseId())) {
   108	            id.set(response.responseId());
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
   113	        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
   114	            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
   115	        }
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
   119	        if (usageMetadata != null) {
   120	            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
   121	                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
   122	                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
   123	                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
   124	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
   125	        }
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
   129	        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
   130	            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
   131	        }
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
   135	        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
   136	        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
   137	        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
   138	        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
   139	            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
   140	        }
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
   144	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   145	        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();
   146	
   147	        return AiMessage.builder()
   148	                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
   149	                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
   150	                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
   151	                .attributes(attributes)
   152	                .build();
   153	    }
   154	}

package dev.langchain4j.model.googleai;

import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.FinishReasonMapper.fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason;
import static dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.PartsAndContentsMapper.fromGPartsToAiMessage;
import static dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason.TOOL_EXECUTION;

import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiCandidate;
import dev.langchain4j.model.googleai.GeminiGenerateContentResponse.GeminiUsageMetadata;
import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;

/**
 * A builder class for constructing streaming responses from Gemini AI model.
 * This class accumulates partial responses and builds a final response.
 */
class GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder {

    private final boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput;
    private final Boolean returnThinking;

    private final StringBuilder contentBuilder;
    private final StringBuilder thoughtBuilder;
    private final Map<String, Object> attributes = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final List<ToolExecutionRequest> functionCalls;

    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    private final AtomicReference<String> modelName = new AtomicReference<>();
    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();

    GeminiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean includeCodeExecutionOutput, Boolean returnThinking) {
        this.includeCodeExecutionOutput = includeCodeExecutionOutput;
        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
        this.contentBuilder = new StringBuilder();
        this.thoughtBuilder = new StringBuilder();
        this.functionCalls = new ArrayList<>();
    }

    record TextAndTools(Optional<String> maybeText, Optional<String> maybeThought, List<ToolExecutionRequest> tools) {}

    /**
     * Appends a partial response to the builder.
     *
     * @param partialResponse the partial response from Gemini AI
     * @return an Optional containing the text of the partial response, or empty if no valid text
     */
    TextAndTools append(GeminiGenerateContentResponse partialResponse) {
        if (partialResponse == null) {
            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
        }

        List<GeminiCandidate> candidates = partialResponse.candidates();
        if (candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty() || candidates.get(0) == null) {
            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
        }

        GeminiCandidate firstCandidate = candidates.get(0);

        updateId(partialResponse);
        updateModelName(partialResponse);
        updateFinishReason(firstCandidate);
        updateTokenUsage(partialResponse.usageMetadata());

        GeminiContent content = firstCandidate.content();
        if (content == null || content.parts() == null) {
            return new TextAndTools(Optional.empty(), Optional.empty(), List.of());
        }

        AiMessage message = fromGPartsToAiMessage(content.parts(), includeCodeExecutionOutput, returnThinking);
        updateContentAndFunctionCalls(message);

        return new TextAndTools(
                Optional.ofNullable(message.text()),
                Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()),
                message.toolExecutionRequests());
    }

    /**
     * Builds the complete response from all accumulated partial responses.
     *
     * @return a Response object containing the complete AiMessage, token usage, and finish reason
     */
    ChatResponse build() {
        AiMessage aiMessage = createAiMessage();
        return ChatResponse.builder()
                .aiMessage(aiMessage)
                .metadata(GoogleAiGeminiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
                        .id(id.get())
                        .modelName(modelName.get())
                        .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
                        .finishReason(aiMessage.hasToolExecutionRequests() ? TOOL_EXECUTION : finishReason.get())
                        .build())
                .build();
    }

    private void updateId(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.responseId())) {
            id.set(response.responseId());
        }
    }

    private void updateModelName(GeminiGenerateContentResponse response) {
        if (!isNullOrBlank(response.modelVersion())) {
            modelName.set(response.modelVersion());
        }
    }

    private void updateTokenUsage(GeminiUsageMetadata usageMetadata) {
        if (usageMetadata != null) {
            TokenUsage tokenUsage = new TokenUsage(
                    usageMetadata.promptTokenCount(),
                    usageMetadata.candidatesTokenCount(),
                    usageMetadata.totalTokenCount());
            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsage);
        }
    }

    private void updateFinishReason(GeminiCandidate candidate) {
        if (candidate.finishReason() != null) {
            this.finishReason.set(fromGFinishReasonToFinishReason(candidate.finishReason()));
        }
    }

    private void updateContentAndFunctionCalls(AiMessage message) {
        Optional.ofNullable(message.text()).ifPresent(contentBuilder::append);
        Optional.ofNullable(message.thinking()).ifPresent(thoughtBuilder::append);
        attributes.putAll(message.attributes());
        if (message.hasToolExecutionRequests()) {
            functionCalls.addAll(message.toolExecutionRequests());
        }
    }

    private AiMessage createAiMessage() {
        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
        String thought = thoughtBuilder.toString();

        return AiMessage.builder()
                .text(text.isEmpty() ? null : text)
                .thinking(thought.isEmpty() ? null : thought)
                .toolExecutionRequests(functionCalls)
                .attributes(attributes)
                .build();
    }
}
